 isse pehle 18 agast se pehle cabinet main pherbadal kii yojana thi, lekin jediu ke saath gathbandhan ko lekar isamen deree ho rahi he

 china ke saath seemaa vivaad ko dekhte hue ek phulatime dephence ministar kii jarurat saaf dekhi ja sakati he

 vahiin smriti irani ke paas bhi do mantralay kaa bhaar he

 in mantralay par najarrel haadason ke baad agar suresh prabhu kii rail mantralay se chuttee hoti he, to piem modi nitin gadakari ko nayaa railmantri niyukt karenge

 saal 2014 main bijepi ke satta main aane ke baad yah vichaar aayaa tha
 However, due to the China dispute, the Ministry of Defense will also be watching
 ab yah dekhnaa dilachasp hoga ki modi arun jetali se koun sa mantralay waapas lete hai
 However, more than one important ministry has already been in the hands of one person
 haalanki ve mantralay aamtaur par ek duusare se jude hote hai
 Finance and Corporate Affairs or the Ministry of Shipping and Road Transport is not a big deal, but if the mismatched departments like finance, defense and textiles, information and broadcasting are given to a single minister, then there is definitely a chance to raise questions
 2019 chunaavon ko dekhte hue faislis pherbadal main raksha mantralay samet 4 bade mantralayon par faisla ho saktaa he

 is pherbadal main 2019 ke loksabhaa chunaavon kaa bhi dhyaan rakhaa jayega

 iske alaava aane vaale vidhansabha chunaavon ko bhi dhyaan main rakhaa jayega

 The High Court has sought a reply from the Commission in 3 days on the petition related to the demand for cancellation of the notification regarding the Election Commission's corporation wards
 court ne kaha he ki ayog apana paksh saaf karte hue bataae ki aakhir kuch essi siton ko general or kuch essi siton ko puri tarah essi nigam vaardon main kis niyam ke tahat tabdeel kiya gaya he
 The High Court will hear the matter again on 16 March
 chunaav ayog kii adhisuchana main dilli ke kuchnigam vaardonko mahilaon or kuch arakshit varg ke liye rakhin gai hai
 Some petitions have been filed in the High Court against this notification

 Political background The first election in Betul Lok Sabha seat was held in 1951
 pehle loksabhaa chunaav main congress ko jeet mili

 saal 1977 ke chunaav main yah seat congress ke haath se nikal gai or bhartiya lokdal ne pehali baar yahaan jeet darj kii thi

 The government has issued an order directing them to mention caste in place of Dalit
 rajya main vidhansabha chunaav ke thik pehle jari hue is aadesh ko congress ne mukhyamantri raman singh kii soshal ejineering kaa hissaa qaraar diya
 The party claims that it is not a circular but a Shigufa
 sarkaar ne jari kiya circularachhattisgarhmen vidhansabha chunaav se kuch maheene pehle rajya sarkaar ne yah circular jari kar anusuchit jati varg ke ek bade samudaay ko saadhane kii koshish kii he
 The state government has banned the use of the word Dalit in all government documents, citing the guidelines of the central government
 chhattisgarhshasan ke saamaanya prashasan vibhaag ne rajya ke sabhi sarkari vibhaagon ko nirdeshit karte hue kaha he ki yah shabd samvidhan main nahin he
 Therefore, it should not be used
 rajya ke gathan ke pehle sanyukt madhyapradesh ke daur main tatkaaleen sarkaar ne 10 farvari 1982 ko notification jari kar harijan shabd par roak lagaai thi
 Punishment was also provided for the use of this word, but how much punishment will be provided for the use of the word Dalit is not clear
 bataaya jaataa he ki mukhyamantri raman singh ke nirdesh ke baad saamaanya prashasan vibhaag ne is paripatr ko jari kar sabhi vibhaagon ko disha-nirdesh die he

 isse anusuchit jati varg ke sammaan main or vruddhi hogi
 Scheduled Caste population increased: In Chhattisgarh, the Scheduled Caste population was 12 percent by the 2011 census
 andaja lagaaya ja rahaa he ki 2018 main isamen 3 fisadi se zyada kii badhotaree hui he
 In the state, 10 out of the total 90 seats are reserved for the scheduled castes
 isamen se 9 siton par bijepi kabiz he
 While one seat is occupied by Congress
 lihaaja, dalit shabd ke istemaal par roak lagaakar rajya kii bijepi sarkaar ne is bade varg ko apane kheme main banaae rakhane kii harsambhav koshish kar rahi he
 The state's BJP government has been carrying out several welfare schemes for the Scheduled Castes for years, but this class felt that the word Dalit in government documents used to defy their honor
 isliye is shabd ko nikaal baahar phenkaa jaae
 CM Raman Singh, in the last phase of his third term, immediately issued an order to keep this class within the BJP by showing the word Dalit out
 congress ne kaha, yah votbank kii raajnneetiudhar, bijepi sarkaar kaa yah faisla congress ko raas nahin aa rahaa
 He believes that this is a shrug-trick of Raman Singh, which has gone for the vote bank
 party ke mutabik vidhansabha chunaav ke chand roj pehle liye gaye is faisle kaa auchity sirf vot bank kii raajnneeti ko hawa dena he
 According to Congress Vice President Ramesh Warliani, BJP has left this new Shigufa
 unhone aarope lagaaya ki 15 saalon main kabhi bhi bijepi ko anusuchit jati varg kaa sammaan najar nahin aayaa
 Now that the assembly elections have come, the party is worried about the respect of this class
 unhone kaha ki yah raman singh kii sochi samajhi soshal ejineering he, lekin bijepi ko iskaa phayda nahin hone vaala
 In Chhattisgarh, BJP and Congress are face to face with preparations for the assembly elections to be held in october-november this year
 kaaryakartaaon ko sakriy karne ke saath-saath partiyaan un jati, samudaay or dharm ke logon ko bhi sakriy karne main jute gai hai, jin virgon kaa vot thok ke bhav unki jholii main girtaa he
 Annoyed with the statement made by Gujarat Chief Minister Narendra Modi about Bihar, Bihar Chief Minister Nitish Kumar, in retaliation, advised Modi to take over his house and said that he (modi) should first see his side
 iske saath hi nitish ne modi ko bihar par tippanee na karne kii salaah dete hue kaha ki bihar apni kamajoriyon se ladate hue vikaas kii raah par aage bad rahaa he
 Nitish also said that we do not comment on others, so if no one else comments on Bihar, it will be good
 ullekhneey he ki rajkot main hui bhaajapa kaaryakarini kii do-divasiy baithak ke samaapan satr ke dauraan ravivaar ko apane sambodhan main modi ne kaha tha ki bihar ke netaaon dwaara jatigat raajnneeti kiye jane ke kaaran yah pradesh pichad gaya
 Modi was pulled by the ruling Janata Dal (united) and opposition party Rashtriya Janata Dal in Bihar for this statement
 bihar vidhanparishad ke sadsy or jad (you) ke pradesh pravaktaa niraj kumaar ne kaha ki modi abhi apni party or gujarat ke bahut saare andruni sankaton se jujh rahe hai, so, aise main vah apane man ke bhav pragat nahin kar rahe hai, balki kahin par nigahen, kahin par nishaanaa laga rahe hai
 Neeraj said that before saying such a thing, Modi should take care that his party is also included in the government here
 niraj ne kaha ki gujarat ko aadharbhoot sanrachana viraasat main mili or bihar kaa adhikansh hissaa baadh or sukhaad se prabhavit rahaa, parantu uske baavjood pradesh ke mukhyamantri nitish kumaar kii kaarykushalta ke boote yahaan badi uplabdhiyaan hasil kii gayi
 Neeraj said that the economic data of the country has proved that a sick state like Bihar is far ahead of Gujarat in terms of growth rate and per capita income, and the glorious history of Bihar in the past, it is a step in the same direction
 is
 jad (you) ke pradesh pravaktaa ke mutabik bihar main in pratikul paristhitiyon ke baavjood jo vikaas dar hasil hui he, vah aadharbhoot sanrachana ke kshetra main hamaare kaaryon kaa nateeja he
 Thanks to financial management, we are taking it forward on the path of development
 unhone kaha ki bihar main jatigat bandhan toote hai
 There were 115 massacres here, which are now closed and there has been an atmosphere of social harmony and communal harmony, some people do not like it
 niraj ne kaha ki nitish aksar kaha karte hai ki saamaajik samarasata evam sampradayik sauhaard hamaari puunji hai or bihar kii 10 karod janata kaa maanav shram he, jisaki badaulat bihar vikaas kar rahaa he or aisa hi bihar main satta main shaamil modi ji kii party bhaajapa ke log bhi kehete hai
 He said that people keep making rhetoric, but the Chief Minister believes in Karma, and is trying to take a sick state like Bihar towards the developed state, this is being accepted by the country and the world
 tippaniyan Asked about Modi's statement about the murder of the banned caste organization Brahmeshwar Mukhiya in Bihar and then his supporters linked to the incidents of sabotage and arson, Neeraj said that if the situation is evaluated, the police would have taken action that day So the social harmony established in the villages with great difficulty could have deteriorated
 unhone kaha ki bihar sarkaar ne sanyam se kaam liya or yah nirnay bhi liya ki jin logon ne bhi us dauraan updrav kiya tha, unhen chihnit kar spidi trial karaayaa jayega, jisase bhavishya main koi aisi himmat nahin kar sake
 At the same time, Nitish advised Modi not to comment on Bihar and said that Bihar is moving forward on the path of development while fighting its weaknesses
 nitish ne yah bhi kaha ki ham dusron par tippanee nahin karte, so, koi or bhi bihar par tippanee na kare to acha hoga

 niraj kaa kahana tha ki ki aisi baat kehane se purv modi ko dhyaan rakhana chahie ki yahaan unki party bhi sarkaar main shaamil he
 Neeraj said that Gujarat inherited the infrastructure and most of Bihar was affected by floods and drought, but despite that due to the efficiency of the Chief Minister of the state, Nitish Kumar, great achievements were made here
 niraj ne kaha ki desh ke aarthik aankadon ne sabit kar diya he ki bihar jaisaa bimaaru rajya vikaas dar or prati vyakti aay ke maamle main gujarat se bahut aage he or bihar kaa jo gauravpurn itihaas purv main rahaa he, yah usee disha main badhata hua kadam he
 According to the JD (U) state spokesperson, the growth rate achieved in Bihar despite these adverse conditions is the result of our actions in the field of infrastructure
